## String References

- **186**: Use the device? [Yes./No.]
- **7635**: Which is real? [The one on the right./The one on the left.]
- **7715**: Which do you choose? [$0./$1./$2.]
- **7716**: Are you sure? [That's the one./No! Wait!]
- **7758**: Touch the crystal? [Yes./No.]
- **7761**: Touch the crystal? [Yes./No.]
- **11858**: @@
- **11868**: You are now able to enjoy a new storyline, Chains of Promathia.
- **11869**: Start Chains of Prromathia? [Yes (View cutscene)./Maybe later.]
- **11870**: Examine the Tales' Beginning in Lower Delkfutt's Tower (H-10) when you wish to start Chains of Promathia.
